Welcome to our Website
Founded in 2015 by Dr. Yamini (PhD, MBA spiritual journey, Astrology – Acharya), Reiki Gyan Organization is a Delhi-based center dedicated to promoting holistic well-being through the combined power of astrology and advanced healing therapies. Our mission is to provide tools, guidance, and energy support to help you achieve complete physical, mental, and spiritual balance Dr. Yamini is a world-renowned astrologer, trusted by clients worldwide for her accurate insights into life’s challenges, past-life connections, and spiritual solutions. By blending astrology with energy healing, she helps individuals understand karmic patterns, overcome blockages, and unlock pathways to success, health, and inner peace.

About Us
Founded in 2015 by Dr. Yamini (PhD Gold Medal, MBA spiritual journey, Astrology – Acharya), Reiki Gyan Organization is a Delhi-based center dedicated to promoting holistic well-being through the combined power of astrology and advanced healing therapies. Our mission is to provide tools, guidance, and energy support to help you achieve complete physical, mental, and spiritual balance Dr. Yamini is a world-renowned astrologer, trusted by clients worldwide for her accurate insights into life’s challenges, past-life connections, and spiritual solutions. By blending astrology with energy healing, she helps individuals understand karmic patterns, overcome blockages, and unlock pathways to success, health, and inner peace.
What We Offer
Gemstones and Crystal Trees for harmonizing all seven chakras
Crystals for protection and spiritual empowerment
Rudraksha Beads in various mukhis for spiritual growth
Healing Bracelets crafted for wealth, focus, emotional healing, and stress relief
Healing Services
Reiki Gyan Organization provides personalized therapies to help with:
Chronic pain relief and physical healing
Stress, anxiety, and emotional harmony
Chakra alignment and deep spiritual cleansing
Our Commitment
We are committed to empowering individuals on their journey to wellness. By combining ancient wisdom with modern healing techniques, Reiki Gyan Organization helps you create a life of balance, positivity, and fulfillment.
I am also a member of RIC – Reiki Council of India

Sciatica Pain Healing Services
Sciatica Pain Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Sciatica Pain Healing Services focus on relieving pain and discomfort caused by sciatic nerve irritation. These services typically include physical therapy to strengthen the muscles supporting the spine and improve flexibility. Techniques such as chiropractic adjustments, acupuncture, and massage therapy may be used to reduce inflammation and alleviate pressure on the sciatic nerve. Heat and cold therapy, along with stretching exercises, help ease muscle tension. Additionally, lifestyle modifications and ergonomic advice are provided to prevent further irritation. By addressing both the symptoms and underlying causes, Sciatica Pain Healing Services aim to restore mobility, reduce pain, and enhance overall quality of life.

Thyroid Healing Services
Thyroid Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Thyroid Healing Services focus on supporting and restoring optimal thyroid function to improve overall health. These services include personalized nutritional counseling to address deficiencies and imbalances, such as incorporating iodine-rich foods and essential nutrients like selenium and zinc. Thyroid-specific supplements and herbal remedies may be recommended to support gland health and hormonal balance. Stress management techniques, including yoga and meditation, are used to reduce cortisol levels that can impact thyroid function. Additionally, lifestyle adjustments and regular monitoring are emphasized to ensure effective management. By addressing dietary, lifestyle, and emotional factors, Thyroid Healing Services aim to enhance thyroid health and overall well-being.

Sleep Stress Healing Services
Sleep Stress Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Sleep Stress Healing Services are designed to address and alleviate stress-related sleep issues to improve overall restfulness and well-being. These services typically include techniques such as relaxation exercises, guided imagery, and cognitive-behavioral therapy for insomnia to address the root causes of sleep disturbances. Stress management strategies, including mindfulness meditation and breathing exercises, help reduce anxiety and promote relaxation before bedtime. Personalized sleep hygiene plans are also provided to establish healthy sleep routines. By combining therapeutic approaches with lifestyle adjustments, Sleep Stress Healing Services aim to enhance sleep quality, reduce stress, and support a healthier, more restful life.

Release Past Healing Services
Release Past Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Release Past Healing Services are designed to help individuals let go of unresolved issues and emotional baggage from the past. These services typically include therapeutic techniques such as guided emotional release, inner child work, and forgiveness practices to address and heal past traumas. Counseling and mindfulness meditation are used to gain insights and cultivate self-compassion. Energy healing practices, like Reiki or chakra balancing, can assist in clearing residual emotional blocks. By focusing on releasing past hurts and fostering personal growth, Release Past Healing Services aim to empower individuals to move forward with a renewed sense of peace and emotional freedom.

Migraine Healing Services
Migraine Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Migraine Healing Services provide targeted support to alleviate and manage migraine symptoms through a holistic approach. These services often include techniques such as acupuncture, which can help reduce the frequency and intensity of migraines, and therapeutic massage to relieve muscle tension and improve circulation. Nutritional counseling may focus on identifying and avoiding migraine triggers while incorporating brain-boosting foods. Stress management strategies, including mindfulness and relaxation exercises, are also emphasized to prevent migraine onset. By addressing physical, dietary, and emotional factors, Migraine Healing Services aim to provide relief, reduce migraine occurrences, and enhance overall quality of life.

Menopause Healing Services
Menopause Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Menopause Healing Services offer holistic support to manage the symptoms and challenges associated with menopause. These services typically include personalized nutritional guidance to balance hormones and support overall health, along with stress management techniques such as yoga and meditation to alleviate mood swings and anxiety. Herbal remedies and supplements may be used to address symptoms like hot flashes and sleep disturbances. Additionally, lifestyle adjustments, including exercise and sleep hygiene practices, are recommended to promote well-being. By providing a comprehensive approach, Menopause Healing Services aim to ease the transition, improve quality of life, and foster balanced, healthy aging.

Joint Bone Healing Services
Joint Bone Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Joint Bone Healing Services provide comprehensive care to support the health and recovery of joints and bones. These services typically include therapies such as physical therapy, which focuses on strengthening exercises and improving mobility, as well as chiropractic adjustments to enhance alignment. Nutritional counseling may be offered to ensure adequate intake of bone-strengthening nutrients like calcium and vitamin D. Additionally, techniques such as massage, acupuncture, and heat therapy can alleviate pain and promote healing. By addressing both the mechanical and nutritional aspects of joint and bone health, these services aim to improve function, reduce discomfort, and enhance overall quality of life.

Immune System Healing Services
Immune System Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Immune System Healing Services focus on strengthening and supporting the body’s natural defenses to enhance overall health. These services often include nutritional guidance, stress reduction techniques, and lifestyle adjustments to boost immune function. Therapies such as herbal remedies, acupuncture, and supplements rich in vitamins and antioxidants are used to fortify the immune system. Regular exercise and proper sleep are also emphasized to maintain optimal immune health. By addressing factors that impact immune resilience, these services help prevent illness, improve recovery times, and promote long-term wellness. Immune System Healing Services offer a holistic approach to achieving a robust and balanced immune response.

Depression Healing Services
Depression Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Depression Healing Services offer holistic approaches to support individuals struggling with depression, aiming to restore mental and emotional balance. These services may include therapies such as counseling, cognitive-behavioral therapy (CBT), meditation, and energy healing to address the root causes of depression. Techniques like mindfulness, breathwork, and nutritional counseling are also used to promote overall well-being. By focusing on the mind-body connection, these services help alleviate symptoms, build resilience, and foster a sense of hope and empowerment. Depression Healing Services provide compassionate support, guiding individuals on their journey toward healing and a more positive outlook on life.

Deep Relaxation Healing Services
Deep Relaxation Healing Services
Link Copied
Get Best Price
Deep Relaxation Healing Services are designed to alleviate stress and tension, promoting a profound sense of calm and well-being. These services often include techniques like guided meditation, aromatherapy, gentle massage, and sound baths, all aimed at soothing the nervous system and quieting the mind. By inducing a state of deep relaxation, these therapies help reduce anxiety, improve sleep, and enhance overall emotional balance. They are ideal for individuals seeking relief from the pressures of daily life or recovering from physical and mental exhaustion. Deep Relaxation Healing Services offer a restorative experience that nurtures both the body and mind.
Read More...

Astrology Services
Leading Wholesaler, Retailer of Marriage Astrology Services and Migraine Healing Services from Delhi.
Marriage Astrology Services
Get Best Price
Marriage Astrology Services provide insights into relationship compatibility and guidance for a harmonious marital life through the study of astrological charts. By examining the birth charts of both partners, astrologers assess the alignment of key planets that influence love, commitment, and emotional connection. These services can predict potential challenges, highlight strengths, and suggest the best times for marriage-related decisions, such as setting a wedding date. Remedies, including rituals and gemstones, may be recommended to enhance compatibility and resolve conflicts. Marriage Astrology Services offer a personalized approach to understanding and nurturing relationships, helping couples build a strong, lasting bond.
Read More...
Request to Call
Migraine Healing Services
Get Best Price
Migraine Healing Services provide targeted support to alleviate and manage migraine symptoms through a holistic approach. These services often include techniques such as acupuncture, which can help reduce the frequency and intensity of migraines, and therapeutic massage to relieve muscle tension and improve circulation. Nutritional counseling may focus on identifying and avoiding migraine triggers while incorporating brain-boosting foods. Stress management strategies, including mindfulness and relaxation exercises, are also emphasized to prevent migraine onset. By addressing physical, dietary, and emotional factors, Migraine Healing Services aim to provide relief, reduce migraine occurrences, and enhance overall quality of life.

Astrology
ABOUT US ASTROLOGY PREDICTIONS ASTROLOGY BY PHONE
Astrology / Jyotish
Astrology is the forecasting of earthly and human events through the observation and interpretation of fixed stars, the Sun, the Moon, and the planets.
How Astrology Helps You
Astrology can guide you in making significant life decisions related to marriage, finance, career, and even health. Many successful people have consulted astrologers to make important choices in their lives.
Vedic Astrology
Vedic horoscopes predict aspects of personal life, describe personalities, and provide advice based on the position of astronomical bodies. To read horoscopes and offer meaningful guidance, a Vedic astrologer must maintain a strong spiritual discipline and approach life’s obstacles from a spiritual perspective.
ASTROLOGY
What is the Vedic System of Astrology?
Rooted in the Vedas—India’s ancient system of knowledge—Vedic astrology is based on the belief that stars and planets hold a powerful influence over human life. According to Hindu teachings, life is meant for spiritual growth, and yearly predictions based on Vedic astrology are considered highly accurate.
Vedic astrology is often referred to as the Eyes of the Vedas (the ancient Indian scriptures). It is a time-tested science of studying celestial bodies through charts, popularly known as a Horoscope or Janam Patrika. By calculating the exact place, date, and time of birth, astrologers read these charts to make in-depth and precise predictions.
How Vedic Astrology Helps You:
* Understand karma and life’s purpose
* Guidance on gemstones and nakshatras (lunar mansions)
* Overcoming bad phases in life
* Marriage, relationships, and family guidance
* Career, job, and business predictions
* Direction and clarity in life decisions
* Kundli (birth chart) analysis for houses and zodiac signs
* Identifying the best dates for important events
* Insights into past, present, and future

LAMA-FERA : A Tibetan art of healing
‘Lama’ means Sadguru and ‘Fera’ means technique so means technique of  Sadguru through which journey from life to death and death to life  becomes easy and peaceful.Lama Fera is being practiced by Tibetan Lamas since ages. Based on Buddha’s process of healing, they developed this technique. Lama Fera is highly powerful Healing technique followed by the Buddhist  and practiced by the Tibetan Lamas. The word Lama means Disciple of lord  Buddha and the word Fera means round or more specifically around the  body with the energy of lord Buddha.The Lama Fera can be practiced with the help of 12 symbols which cannot be reveled and as they use to benefit people.The  symbols of Lama Fera have amplitude power to serve highest level of  negative energy. The method of its healing is quite different from Reiki  and other types of healing therapies used in modern society.It  helps to coherent the negative energy and unwanted issues in the health  and also helps you to gain awareness, knowledge and enlightenment i.e.  through the power of lord Buddha.There are some parameters for  learning Lama Fera,  Our whole plane is composed of physical body, etheric body, mental body and emotional body Also reciting the sacred mantras for lord Buddha.  One can learn this technique of healing in couple of days ,  have to be truly dedicated towards the process and should follow them  one after the other. Our seven major centers of light i.e. Chakras governs this flow of  energy. When this energy is blocked due to psychic attacks, black magic, spell, entities, Karmic blockages, critical illness, financial blockages can be removed.  entity attachments, negative consequences happens such as ill health,  mental problems, financial blockage and in some cases accidents too.

TAROT CARD ONLINE
Tarot Information
Reiki Gyan Org  offers you an exceptional fortune telling experience. Using  the Online Tarot Card, you can see your future based on the cards you  have drawn.
My name is Yamini Sharma and I have been practicing the fortune telling  arts for almost 11 years. I wanted to share my knowledge of tarot  reading by offering a completely free draw using the 78 tarot Card.
This experience is based on research conducted in the  including YOU! NO
The 78-card tarot deck used by esoteric has two distinct parts:
The Major Arcana (greater secrets), or trump cards, consists of 22 cards without suits: ...
The Minor Arcana (lesser secrets) consists of 56 cards, divided into four suits of 14 cards
I believe I can help you understand the hidden meaning of things.  While many people believe that Tarot will tell you the future, making predictions, want to create your ideal future and manifest your  goals, your inner wisdom  And you  can discover how to make positive changes  you can manifest your goals and your dreams come a true in the future

Healing
REIKI NATURAL HEALING
Reiki Healer use a technique called healing or hands healing through which “Universal Energy” flows to recipient's major organs or major chakras. It is transferred through the palms of the practitioner to the patient in order to encourage emotional or physical healing.
About Reiki Gyan Healing Treatments
Reiki is a meditative practice that promotes relaxation, reduces stress and anxiety and promotes a positive mental state through gentle touch. Reiki is safe way to compliment for your medical needs. You might feel more relaxed or less stressed out. If you’re getting Reiki  for a health condition, you’ll still need to follow your treatment and  see your doctor like you usually do. Reiki doesn’t replace your regular  medical care.   Reiki Treatment works directly on the problem and  condition . Benefits of reiki Treatments are:
Poor Self Confidence
Colds/ Immune system
Release  Past
Balance all Chakras
Energy body Support
Chronic Pain
Chronic Back Pain
Joints Bone Pain
Depression
Migraine
Exam Concentration /memory
Muscular Dystrophy
Deep Relaxation
Fitness
Sleep stress balanced
Positivity Thoughts
Coccyx Pain
Joints tissue
Spleen
Pancreas Diabetes
Blood Circulation
Hormonal Balance
Menopause
Gastro Problems
Thyroid
Sciatica Pain
Protection Healing
Exam Concentration
Tailbone  Pain
FOR NATURAL HEALING
Reiki Natural healing is a form of complementary therapy relating to energy healing.  Proponents say that it works with the energy fields around the body and  involves the transfer of universal energy from the practitioner’s palms  to the client.  You can explain what Reiki treatment involves, its reported health benefits, and the medical opinions surrounding it.   If you are living with certain health conditions may be interested in trying Reiki alongside their regular treatment.

Welcome to our Website
Founded in 2015 by Dr. Yamini (PhD, MBA spiritual journey, Astrology – Acharya), Reiki Gyan Organization is a Delhi-based center dedicated to promoting holistic well-being through the combined power of astrology and advanced healing therapies. Our mission is to provide tools, guidance, and energy support to help you achieve complete physical, mental, and spiritual balance Dr. Yamini is a world-renowned astrologer, trusted by clients worldwide for her accurate insights into life’s challenges, past-life connections, and spiritual solutions. By blending astrology with energy healing, she helps individuals understand karmic patterns, overcome blockages, and unlock pathways to success, health, and inner peace.
